New String: ```
// Page principale de l'assistant Block Puzzle — jeu réel avec effacement de lignes
import React, { useState, useCallback, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import type { Grid, BlockInstance, Suggestion, CellState } from '@/types/types';
import {
  generateSuggestions,
  suggestNextBlocks,
  suggestOneBlock,
  findBossSlot,
  computeBossReservation,
  reservationToCellSet,
} from '@/lib/predictionEngine';
import type { ClearMemory, BossReservation } from '@/lib/predictionEngine';
import { getInstanceShape, gridToBool, canPlace, applyPlacementWithClears } from '@/lib/blockUtils';
import { DragProvider } from '@/contexts/DragContext';
import { GameGrid } from '@/components/game/GameGrid';
import { HandSelector } from '@/components/game/HandSelector';
import { SuggestionsPanel } from '@/components/game/SuggestionsPanel';
import { GridToolbar } from '@/components/game/GridToolbar';
import { ThemeConfigPanel } from '@/components/game/ThemeConfigPanel';
import { ThemeProvider, useTheme } from '@/contexts/ThemeContext';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import { LayoutGrid, Info, Puzzle, Sparkles, Hand, Trophy, Zap } from 'lucide-react';

const GRID_SIZE = 8;
const MAX_MEMORY = 5; // garder les 5 derniers coups en mémoire

function createEmptyGrid(): Grid {
  return Array.from({ length: GRID_SIZE }, () =>
    Array.from({ length: GRID_SIZE }, (): CellState => ({
      occupied: false,
      color: null,
    }))
  );
}

const BlockPuzzleAssistant: React.FC = () => {
  const { theme } = useTheme();

  const [grid, setGrid] = useState<Grid>(createEmptyGrid);
  const [paintMode, setPaintMode] = useState<'paint' | 'erase'>('paint');
  const [selectedColor, setSelectedColor] = useState(theme.blockColors[0]);
  const [hand, setHand] = useState<Array<BlockInstance | null>>([null, null, null]);
  const [suggestions, setSuggestions] = useState<Record<number, Suggestion[]>>({});
  const [hoveredSuggestion, setHoveredSuggestion] = useState<Suggestion | null>(null);
  const [isAnalyzing, setIsAnalyzing] = useState(false);
  const [highlightedSlot, setHighlightedSlot] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const [hasAnalyzed, setHasAnalyzed] = useState(false);
  const [kbSlot, setKbSlot] = useState<number | null>(null);

  // ── Score & animation ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const [score, setScore] = useState(0);
  const [scoreBump, setScoreBump] = useState(false);
  const [explodingCells, setExplodingCells] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());
  const [scorePopup, setScorePopup] = useState<{ value: number; key: number } | null>(null);
  const popupKeyRef = useRef(0);
  const explodeTimerRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);

  // ── Stratégie Boss ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const [bossSlot, setBossSlot] = useState<number>(1);
  const [bossReservation, setBossReservation] = useState<BossReservation | null>(null);
  const [clearMemory, setClearMemory] = useState<ClearMemory[]>([]);
  const turnCountRef = useRef(0);

  // Recalcule le boss + sa zone réservée à chaque changement de main ou grille
  const recomputeBoss = useCallback(
    (currentGrid: Grid, currentHand: Array<BlockInstance | null>, currentMemory: ClearMemory[]) => {
      const newBossSlot = findBossSlot(currentHand);
      setBossSlot(newBossSlot);
      const bossBlock = currentHand[newBossSlot];
      if (!bossBlock) {
        setBossReservation(null);
        return;
      }
      const reservation = computeBossReservation(currentGrid, bossBlock, newBossSlot, currentMemory);
      setBossReservation(reservation);
    },
    []
  );

  // Recalculer le boss quand la main change
  useEffect(() => {
    recomputeBoss(grid, hand, clearMemory);
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, [hand]);

  const occupiedCount = grid.flat().filter(c => c.occupied).length;

  // ── Peinture manuelle ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleCellClick = useCallback(
    (row: number, col: number) => {
      if (kbSlot !== null) return;
      setGrid(prev => {
        const next = prev.map(r => r.map(c => ({ ...c })));
        if (paintMode === 'erase') {
          next[row][col] = { occupied: false, color: null };
        } else {
          const cell = next[row][col];
          if (cell.occupied && cell.color === selectedColor) {
            next[row][col] = { occupied: false, color: null };
          } else {
            next[row][col] = { occupied: true, color: selectedColor };
          }
        }
        return next;
      });
      if (hasAnalyzed) { setSuggestions({}); setHasAnalyzed(false); }
    },
    [paintMode, selectedColor, hasAnalyzed, kbSlot]
  );

  const handleSlotChange = useCallback(
    (slot: 0 | 1 | 2, block: BlockInstance | null) => {
      setHand(prev => {
        const next = [...prev] as Array<BlockInstance | null>;
        next[slot] = block;
        return next;
      });
      setSuggestions({});
      setHasAnalyzed(false);
    },
    []
  );

  // ── Shuffle d'un bloc non-boss ────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleShuffleSlot = useCallback(
    (slot: 0 | 1 | 2) => {
      if (slot === bossSlot) return; // le boss ne se shufflerait pas
      const excludeIds = hand
        .filter((b): b is BlockInstance => b !== null)
        .map(b => b.definition.id);
      const newBlock = suggestOneBlock(
        grid,
        theme.blockColors,
        excludeIds,
        bossReservation,
        clearMemory
      );
      if (!newBlock) {
        toast.warning('Aucun bloc compatible trouvé', {
          description: 'La grille ne permet pas d\'autres blocs en ce moment.',
        });
        return;
      }
      // Appliquer la couleur du slot
      const coloredBlock: BlockInstance = {
        ...newBlock,
        color: theme.blockColors[slot] || newBlock.color,
      };
      setHand(prev => {
        const next = [...prev] as Array<BlockInstance | null>;
        next[slot] = coloredBlock;
        return next;
      });
      setSuggestions({});
      setHasAnalyzed(false);
      toast.success(`🔀 Bloc ${slot + 1} remplacé par ${coloredBlock.definition.name}`, {
        description: 'Nouveau bloc sélectionné par l\'IA.',
        duration: 2000,
      });
    },
    [bossSlot, hand, grid, theme.blockColors, bossReservation, clearMemory]
  );

  // ── Analyse ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleAnalyze = useCallback(() => {
    const hasBlocks = hand.some(Boolean);
    if (!hasBlocks) {
      toast.info('Ajoutez au moins un bloc dans votre main', {
        description: 'Utilisez les 3 slots ci-dessous pour sélectionner vos blocs.',
      });
      return;
    }
    setIsAnalyzing(true);
    setTimeout(() => {
      try {
        const result = generateSuggestions(grid, hand, 3, bossReservation, clearMemory);
        setSuggestions(result);
        setHasAnalyzed(true);
        const total = Object.values(result).flat().length;
        if (total === 0) {
          toast.warning('Aucun placement possible', { description: 'La grille est trop remplie.' });
        } else {
          toast.success(`${total} suggestion${total > 1 ? 's' : ''} trouvée${total > 1 ? 's' : ''}`, {
            description: 'Survolez une carte pour prévisualiser le placement.',
          });
        }
      } catch {
        toast.error("Erreur lors de l'analyse");
      } finally {
        setIsAnalyzing(false);
      }
    }, 50);
  }, [grid, hand, bossReservation, clearMemory]);

  // ── Effacer la grille ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleClearGrid = useCallback(() => {
    setGrid(createEmptyGrid());
    setSuggestions({});
    setHasAnalyzed(false);
    setHoveredSuggestion(null);
    setKbSlot(null);
    setScore(0);
    setExplodingCells(new Set());
    setScorePopup(null);
    setBossReservation(null);
    setClearMemory([]);
    turnCountRef.current = 0;
    toast.info('Grille effacée');
  }, []);

  const handleHoverSuggestion = useCallback((s: Suggestion | null) => {
    setHoveredSuggestion(s);
    if (!s) { setHighlightedSlot(null); return; }
    const entry = Object.entries(suggestions).find(([, arr]) => arr.some(sg => sg.id === s.id));
    setHighlightedSlot(entry ? parseInt(entry[0]) : null);
  }, [suggestions]);

  // ── Recharger la main si tous les slots sont vides ──────────────────────
  const refillHandIfEmpty = useCallback(
    (updatedHand: Array<BlockInstance | null>, currentGrid: Grid, currentMemory: ClearMemory[]): Array<BlockInstance | null> => {
      const allEmpty = updatedHand.every(b => b === null);
      if (!allEmpty) return updatedHand;
      const colors = theme.blockColors;
      const suggested = suggestNextBlocks(currentGrid, colors, 3);
      // suggestNextBlocks garantit déjà [petit, grand(boss), moyen]
      toast.info("✨ Nouvelle main générée par l'IA", {
        description: 'Bloc central = 👑 Boss (le plus grand). Réservation mise à jour.',
        duration: 3000,
      });
      // Recalculer le boss avec la nouvelle main dans la prochaine update
      setTimeout(() => recomputeBoss(currentGrid, suggested as Array<BlockInstance | null>, currentMemory), 0);
      return suggested as Array<BlockInstance | null>;
    },
    [theme.blockColors, recomputeBoss]
  );

  // ── Logique centrale : placer un bloc + effacer lignes/cols + score ───────
  const triggerPlacementResult = useCallback(
    (
      newGrid: Grid,
      result: { clearedLines: number[]; clearedCols: number[]; scoreGained: number; cellsFreed: number },
      newHand: Array<BlockInstance | null> | null,
      newMemory: ClearMemory[]
    ) => {
      const { clearedLines, clearedCols, scoreGained, cellsFreed } = result;
      const combos = clearedLines.length + clearedCols.length;

      const toExplode = new Set<string>();
      for (const r of clearedLines) {
        for (let c = 0; c < GRID_SIZE; c++) toExplode.add(`${r},${c}`);
      }
      for (const col of clearedCols) {
        for (let r = 0; r < GRID_SIZE; r++) toExplode.add(`${r},${col}`);
      }

      setGrid(newGrid);

      if (toExplode.size > 0) {
        setExplodingCells(toExplode);
        if (explodeTimerRef.current) clearTimeout(explodeTimerRef.current);
        explodeTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
          setExplodingCells(new Set());
          if (newHand) {
            setHand(newHand);
          }
          // Recalculer boss après effacement + nouvelle main
          recomputeBoss(newGrid, newHand ?? [], newMemory);
          setSuggestions({});
          setHasAnalyzed(false);
        }, 500);
      } else {
        if (newHand) setHand(newHand);
        recomputeBoss(newGrid, newHand ?? [], newMemory);
        setSuggestions({});
        setHasAnalyzed(false);
      }

      if (scoreGained > 0) {
        setScore(prev => prev + scoreGained);
        setScoreBump(true);
        setTimeout(() => setScoreBump(false), 400);
        popupKeyRef.current += 1;
        setScorePopup({ value: scoreGained, key: popupKeyRef.current });
        setTimeout(() => setScorePopup(null), 1100);
        const comboMsg = combos > 1 ? ` (×${combos} combo !)` : '';
        toast.success(`🎉 ${cellsFreed} cases libérées${comboMsg}`, {
          description: `+${scoreGained} points`,
          duration: 2000,
        });
      }
    },
    [recomputeBoss]
  );

  // Construit la nouvelle mémoire après un placement
  const buildNewMemory = useCallback(
    (clearedLines: number[], clearedCols: number[]): ClearMemory[] => {
      if (clearedLines.length === 0 && clearedCols.length === 0) return clearMemory;
      turnCountRef.current += 1;
      const newEntry: ClearMemory = {
        lines: clearedLines,
        cols: clearedCols,
        turn: turnCountRef.current,
      };
      const updated = [...clearMemory, newEntry];
      // Garder seulement les MAX_MEMORY derniers souvenirs
      const trimmed = updated.slice(-MAX_MEMORY);
      setClearMemory(trimmed);
      return trimmed;
    },
    [clearMemory]
  );

  // ── Appliquer une suggestion ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleApplySuggestion = useCallback((suggestion: Suggestion) => {
    const shape = getInstanceShape(suggestion.blockInstance);
    const result = applyPlacementWithClears(
      grid,
      shape,
      suggestion.position.row,
      suggestion.position.col,
      suggestion.blockInstance.color
    );
    const slotEntry = Object.entries(suggestions).find(([, arr]) =>
      arr.some(s => s.id === suggestion.id)
    );
    const slotIndex = slotEntry ? parseInt(slotEntry[0]) : -1;
    const updatedHand = [...hand] as Array<BlockInstance | null>;
    if (slotIndex >= 0) updatedHand[slotIndex] = null;
    const newMemory = buildNewMemory(result.clearedLines, result.clearedCols);
    const finalHand = refillHandIfEmpty(updatedHand, result.newGrid, newMemory);
    triggerPlacementResult(result.newGrid, result, finalHand, newMemory);
    setHoveredSuggestion(null);
  }, [grid, hand, suggestions, refillHandIfEmpty, triggerPlacementResult, buildNewMemory]);

  // ── Placer un bloc (drag, clavier) ───────────────────────────────────────
  const placeBlock = useCallback(
    (block: BlockInstance, slotIndex: number, anchorRow: number, anchorCol: number): boolean => {
      const shape = getInstanceShape(block);
      const boolGrid = gridToBool(grid);
      if (!canPlace(boolGrid, shape, anchorRow, anchorCol)) return false;
      const result = applyPlacementWithClears(grid, shape, anchorRow, anchorCol, block.color);
      const updatedHand = [...hand] as Array<BlockInstance | null>;
      if (slotIndex >= 0) updatedHand[slotIndex] = null;
      const newMemory = buildNewMemory(result.clearedLines, result.clearedCols);
      const finalHand = refillHandIfEmpty(updatedHand, result.newGrid, newMemory);
      triggerPlacementResult(result.newGrid, result, finalHand, newMemory);
      return true;
    },
    [grid, hand, refillHandIfEmpty, triggerPlacementResult, buildNewMemory]
  );

  // ── Drop depuis la Main ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleBlockDropped = useCallback(
    (block: BlockInstance, slotIndex: number, row: number, col: number) => {
      const ok = placeBlock(block, slotIndex, row, col);
      if (!ok) {
        toast.error('Placement invalide', { description: 'Ce bloc ne peut pas être placé ici.' });
      } else {
        toast.success(`Bloc ${block.definition.name} placé !`, {
          description: `Ligne ${row + 1}, colonne ${col + 1}`,
        });
      }
    },
    [placeBlock]
  );

  // ── Mode clavier ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleKeyDown = useCallback(
    (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
      if (e.target instanceof HTMLInputElement || e.target instanceof HTMLTextAreaElement) return;
      if (e.key === '1' && hand[0]) { setKbSlot(0); e.preventDefault(); }
      else if (e.key === '2' && hand[1]) { setKbSlot(1); e.preventDefault(); }
      else if (e.key === '3' && hand[2]) { setKbSlot(2); e.preventDefault(); }
      else if (e.key === 'Escape') { setKbSlot(null); }
    },
    [hand]
  );

  const handleKeyboardPlace = useCallback(
    (row: number, col: number) => {
      if (kbSlot === null) return;
      const block = hand[kbSlot];
      if (!block) return;
      const ok = placeBlock(block, kbSlot, row, col);
      if (ok) {
        toast.success(`Bloc ${block.definition.name} placé !`, {
          description: `Clavier — Ligne ${row + 1}, colonne ${col + 1}`,
        });
        setKbSlot(null);
      } else {
        toast.error('Placement invalide', { description: 'Choisissez une position libre.' });
      }
    },
    [kbSlot, hand, placeBlock]
  );

  // Cellules réservées pour l'overlay boss
  const reservedZoneCells = reservationToCellSet(bossReservation);
  const bossBlock = hand[bossSlot];
  const bossColor = bossBlock?.color ?? theme.accentColor;

  return (
    <div
      className="flex flex-col min-h-screen bg-background"
      onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
      tabIndex={-1}
    >
      {/* ── Header ── */}
      <header className="flex-shrink-0 border-b border-border bg-card/90 backdrop-blur-sm sticky top-0 z-10 shadow-sm">
        <div className="max-w-screen-xl mx-auto px-4 py-2.5 flex items-center justify-between gap-4">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2.5 min-w-0">
            <div
              className="w-8 h-8 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0"
              style={{
                background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${theme.accentColor}30, ${theme.accentColor}15)`,
                border: `1px solid ${theme.accentColor}50`,
              }}
            >
              <Puzzle className="h-4 w-4" style={{ color: theme.accentColor }} />
            </div>
            <div className="min-w-0">
              <h1 className="text-sm font-bold text-foreground leading-tight truncate">
                Block Puzzle — Assistant IA
              </h1>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground hidden sm:block">
                Prédiction intelligente des meilleurs coups
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-shrink-0">
            {/* Indicateur mémoire */}
            {clearMemory.length > 0 && (
              <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs hidden md:flex gap-1 font-mono"
                style={{ borderColor: `${theme.accentColor}40`, color: theme.accentColor }}>
                🧠 {clearMemory.length} coup{clearMemory.length > 1 ? 's' : ''} mémorisé{clearMemory.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}
              </Badge>
            )}
            {/* Score */}
            <div
              className={`flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md border ${scoreBump ? 'animate-score-bump' : ''}`}
              style={{
                borderColor: `${theme.accentColor}50`,
                background: `${theme.accentColor}10`,
              }}
            >
              <Trophy className="h-3.5 w-3.5" style={{ color: theme.accentColor }} />
              <span
                className="text-sm font-bold font-mono tabular-nums"
                style={{ color: theme.accentColor }}
              >
                {score.toLocaleString()}
              </span>
            </div>
            <Badge variant="secondary" className="text-xs hidden sm:flex font-mono"
              style={{ borderColor: `${theme.accentColor}40` }}>
              8 × 8
            </Badge>
            <ThemeConfigPanel />
          </div>
        </div>
      </header>

      {/* ── Layout principal ── */}
      <main className="flex-1 max-w-screen-xl mx-auto w-full px-4 py-4 min-w-0">
        <div className="flex flex-col lg:flex-row gap-4">

          {/* ═══ Colonne centrale ═══ */}
          <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 flex flex-col gap-3">

            {/* Barre d'outils */}
            <div className="bg-card rounded-md border border-border p-3 shadow-sm">
              <GridToolbar
                selectedColor={selectedColor}
                onColorChange={setSelectedColor}
                mode={paintMode}
                onModeChange={setPaintMode}
                onClearGrid={handleClearGrid}
                occupiedCount={occupiedCount}
                onAnalyze={handleAnalyze}
                isAnalyzing={isAnalyzing}
              />
            </div>

            {/* Grille 8×8 */}
            <div className="bg-card rounded-md border border-border p-4 shadow-sm">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
                <LayoutGrid className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground flex-shrink-0" />
                <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground">Plateau de jeu</span>
                {explodingCells.size > 0 && (
                  <span className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs font-medium ml-1"
                    style={{ color: theme.accentColor }}>
                    <Zap className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
                    Explosion !
                  </span>
                )}
                {bossReservation && (
                  <span className="text-xs ml-1 hidden sm:inline" style={{ color: bossColor }}>
                    👑 Zone Boss réservée
                  </span>
                )}
                <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs ml-auto font-mono">
                  {occupiedCount}/64
                </Badge>
              </div>
              <div className="overflow-x-auto w-full flex justify-center">
                <GameGrid
                  grid={grid}
                  onCellClick={handleCellClick}
                  selectedColor={selectedColor}
                  hoveredSuggestion={hoveredSuggestion}
                  isEditing={kbSlot === null}
                  onBlockDropped={handleBlockDropped}
                  keyboardBlock={kbSlot !== null ? hand[kbSlot] : null}
                  keyboardSlot={kbSlot}
                  onKeyboardPlace={handleKeyboardPlace}
                  onKeyboardCancel={() => setKbSlot(null)}
                  explodingCells={explodingCells}
                  scorePopup={scorePopup}
                  reservedZoneCells={reservedZoneCells}
                  bossColor={bossColor}
                />
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* ══ Main du joueur ══ */}
            <div className="bg-card rounded-md border border-border p-4 shadow-sm">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
                <Hand className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground flex-shrink-0" />
                <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground">Ma main</span>
                <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground ml-1 hidden sm:inline">
                  — glissez un bloc vers la grille
                </span>
                <Badge variant="secondary" className="text-xs ml-auto">
                  {hand.filter(Boolean).length}/3
                </Badge>
              </div>
              <HandSelector
                hand={hand}
                onSlotChange={handleSlotChange}
                highlightedSlot={highlightedSlot}
                keyboardSelectedSlot={kbSlot}
                onKeyboardSelectSlot={setKbSlot}
                bossSlot={bossSlot}
                onShuffleSlot={handleShuffleSlot}
              />
            </div>

            {/* Aide rapide */}
            <div className="flex items-start gap-2 p-3 rounded-md border border-border bg-muted/30 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
              <Info className="h-3.5 w-3.5 mt-0.5 flex-shrink-0 text-primary/60" />
              <p className="text-pretty">
                <strong className="text-foreground">Comment jouer :</strong>{' '}
                ① <strong className="text-foreground">Glissez</strong> un bloc de «&nbsp;Ma main&nbsp;» vers la grille.{' '}
                ② Le <strong className="text-yellow-600 dark:text-yellow-400">👑 Boss</strong> (bloc du milieu, le plus grand) a une{' '}
                <strong className="text-foreground">zone réservée</strong> (pointillés sur la grille) — l'IA l'utilise en dernier recours.{' '}
                ③ Utilisez <strong className="text-foreground">🔀 Changer</strong> sur les blocs gauche/droite pour demander un remplaçant IA.{' '}
                ④ Touche{' '}
                <kbd className="px-1 py-0.5 rounded bg-muted font-mono text-[10px]">1</kbd>
                <kbd className="px-1 py-0.5 rounded bg-muted font-mono text-[10px] mx-0.5">2</kbd>
                <kbd className="px-1 py-0.5 rounded bg-muted font-mono text-[10px]">3</kbd>{' '}
                + flèches + <kbd className="px-1 py-0.5 rounded bg-muted font-mono text-[10px]">Entrée</kbd>{' '}
                pour le mode clavier.
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* ═══ Sidebar droite ═══ */}
          <div className="lg:w-80 xl:w-96 flex-shrink-0">
            <div
              className="bg-card rounded-md border border-border shadow-sm p-4 flex flex-col lg:sticky lg:top-[60px]"
              style={{ maxHeight: 'calc(100vh - 80px)' }}
            >
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3 flex-shrink-0">
                <Sparkles className="h-4 w-4 flex-shrink-0" style={{ color: theme.accentColor }} />
                <span className="text-sm font-bold text-foreground">Suggestions IA</span>
                {hasAnalyzed && (
                  <Badge variant="secondary" className="text-xs ml-auto"
                    style={{ borderColor: `${theme.accentColor}40`, color: theme.accentColor }}>
                    {Object.values(suggestions).flat().length} idées
                  </Badge>
                )}
              </div>
              <div
                className="h-0.5 w-full rounded-full mb-3 flex-shrink-0"
                style={{ background: `linear-gradient(90deg, ${theme.accentColor}60, transparent)` }}
              />
              {/* Info boss dans la sidebar */}
              {bossReservation && bossBlock && (
                <div className="mb-3 flex-shrink-0 p-2 rounded-md border text-xs"
                  style={{ borderColor: `${bossColor}40`, background: `${bossColor}08` }}>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 font-medium mb-0.5" style={{ color: bossColor }}>
                    <span>👑 Boss — {bossBlock.definition.name}</span>
                    <Badge className="text-[9px] px-1 h-4 ml-auto" style={{ background: `${bossColor}20`, color: bossColor, border: `1px solid ${bossColor}40` }}>
                      {bossBlock.definition.size} cases
                    </Badge>
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-muted-foreground leading-snug">
                    Zone réservée à L{bossReservation.row + 1}&nbsp;C{bossReservation.col + 1}.
                    Les blocs gauche/droite sont suggérés pour <em>ne pas bloquer</em> cette zone.
                  </p>
                </div>
              )}
              <div className="flex-1 min-h-0">
                <SuggestionsPanel
                  suggestions={suggestions}
                  hand={hand.map((_, i) => ({ slot: i }))}
                  isLoading={isAnalyzing}
                  hoveredSuggestion={hoveredSuggestion}
                  onHoverSuggestion={handleHoverSuggestion}
                  onApplySuggestion={handleApplySuggestion}
                />
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

        </div>
      </main>
    </div>
  );
};

const BlockPuzzlePage: React.FC = () => (
  <ThemeProvider>
    <DragProvider>
      <BlockPuzzleAssistant />
    </DragProvider>
  </ThemeProvider>
);

export default BlockPuzzlePage;
```

     1 // Contexte de thème pour l'application
     2 import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect } from 'react';
     3 import type { ThemeConfig } from '@/types/types';
     4 import { DEFAULT_THEME } from '@/types/types';
     5 
     6 interface ThemeContextValue {
     7   theme: ThemeConfig;
     8   updateTheme: (partial: Partial<ThemeConfig>) => void;
     9   resetTheme: () => void;
    10 }
    11 
    12 const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextValue | null>(null);
    13 
    14 export const ThemeProvider: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
    15   const [theme, setTheme] = useState<ThemeConfig>(() => {
    16     try {
    17       const saved = localStorage.getItem('blockpuzzle-theme');
    18       return saved ? { ...DEFAULT_THEME, ...JSON.parse(saved) } : DEFAULT_THEME;
    19     } catch {
    20       return DEFAULT_THEME;
    21     }
    22   });
    23 
    24   useEffect(() => {
    25     // Appliquer le mode dark/light
    26     if (theme.isDark) {
    27       document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
    28     } else {
    29       document.documentElement.classList.remove('dark');
    30     }
    31 
    32     // Appliquer la couleur d'accent personnalisée
    33     const hex = theme.accentColor;
    34     const hsl = hexToHsl(hex);
    35     if (hsl) {
    36       document.documentElement.style.setProperty(
    37         '--primary',
    38         `${hsl.h} ${hsl.s}% ${hsl.l}%`
    39       );
    40       document.documentElement.style.setProperty(
    41         '--ring',
    42         `${hsl.h} ${hsl.s}% ${hsl.l}%`
    43       );
    44     }
    45 
    46     // Sauvegarder
    47     localStorage.setItem('blockpuzzle-theme', JSON.stringify(theme));
    48   }, [theme]);
    49 
    50   const updateTheme = (partial: Partial<ThemeConfig>) => {
    51     setTheme(prev => ({ ...prev, ...partial }));
    52   };
    53 
    54   const resetTheme = () => setTheme(DEFAULT_THEME);
    55 
    56   return (
    57     <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, updateTheme, resetTheme }}>
    58       {children}
    59     </ThemeContext.Provider>
    60   );
    61 };
    62 
    63 export const useTheme = (): ThemeContextValue => {
    64   const ctx = useContext(ThemeContext);
    65   if (!ctx) throw new Error('useTheme doit être utilisé dans ThemeProvider');
    66   return ctx;
    67 };
    68 
    69 // Convertir hex en HSL
    70 function hexToHsl(hex: string): { h: number; s: number; l: number } | null {
    71   const result = /^#?([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})$/i.exec(hex);
    72   if (!result) return null;
    73 
    74   const r = parseInt(result[1], 16) / 255;
    75   const g = parseInt(result[2], 16) / 255;
    76   const b = parseInt(result[3], 16) / 255;
    77 
    78   const max = Math.max(r, g, b), min = Math.min(r, g, b);
    79   let h = 0, s = 0;
    80   const l = (max + min) / 2;
    81 
    82   if (max !== min) {
    83     const d = max - min;
    84     s = l > 0.5 ? d / (2 - max - min) : d / (max + min);
    85     switch (max) {
    86       case r: h = ((g - b) / d + (g < b ? 6 : 0)) / 6; break;
    87       case g: h = ((b - r) / d + 2) / 6; break;
    88       case b: h = ((r - g) / d + 4) / 6; break;
    89     }
    90   }
    91 
    92   return {
    93     h: Math.round(h * 360),
    94     s: Math.round(s * 100),
    95     l: Math.round(l * 100),
    96   };
    97 }
    98

   281     <Badge variant="secondary" className="text-[9px] px-1 py-0 h-4">{definition.size}</Badge>
   282   </button>
   283 );

   285 // Composant principal: main du joueur (3 slots)
   286 interface HandSelectorProps {
   287   hand: Array<BlockInstance | null>;
   288   onSlotChange: (slot: 0 | 1 | 2, block: BlockInstance | null) => void;
   289   highlightedSlot?: number | null;
   290   keyboardSelectedSlot?: number | null;
   291   onKeyboardSelectSlot?: (slot: number | null) => void;
   292   bossSlot?: number;
   293   onShuffleSlot?: (slot: 0 | 1 | 2) => void;
   294 }
   295 
   296 export const HandSelector: React.FC<HandSelectorProps> = ({
   297   hand,
   298   onSlotChange,
   299   highlightedSlot,
   300   keyboardSelectedSlot,
   301   bossSlot = 1,
   302   onShuffleSlot,
   303 }) => {
   304   const handleRotate = (slot: 0 | 1 | 2) => {
   305     const block = hand[slot];
   306     if (!block) return;
   307     const rotations: Array<0 | 90 | 180 | 270> = [0, 90, 180, 270];
   308     const currentIdx = rotations.indexOf(block.rotation);
   309     const nextRotation = rotations[(currentIdx + 1) % 4];
   310     onSlotChange(slot, { ...block, rotation: nextRotation });
   311   };
   312 
   313   const handleFlip = (slot: 0 | 1 | 2) => {
   314     const block = hand[slot];
   315     if (!block) return;
   316     onSlotChange(slot, { ...block, flipped: !block.flipped });
   317   };
   318 
   319   return (
   320     <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
   321       <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
   322         {([0, 1, 2] as const).map(slot => (
   323           <HandSlot
   324             key={slot}
   325             slot={slot}
   326             block={hand[slot]}
   327             onSelect={(s, b) => onSlotChange(s, b)}
   328             onRemove={s => onSlotChange(s, null)}
   329             onRotate={handleRotate}
   330             onFlip={handleFlip}
   331             isBoss={slot === bossSlot}
   332             onShuffle={slot !== bossSlot ? onShuffleSlot : undefined}
   333             isHighlighted={highlightedSlot === slot}
   334             isKeyboardSelected={keyboardSelectedSlot === slot}
   335           />
   336         ))}
   337       </div>
   338       {keyboardSelectedSlot !== null && keyboardSelectedSlot !== undefined && (
   339         <div className="text-xs text-primary text-center animate-suggestion-in">
   340           ⌨️ Bloc {keyboardSelectedSlot + 1} sélectionné — Utilisez les flèches sur la grille, Entrée pour placer, Échap pour annuler
   341         </div>
   342       )}
   343       {(keyboardSelectedSlot === null || keyboardSelectedSlot === undefined) && (
   344         <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground text-center">
   345           Glissez un bloc vers la grille ou appuyez sur{' '}
   346           <kbd className="px-1 py-0.5 rounded bg-muted font-mono text-[10px]">1</kbd>
   347           <kbd className="px-1 py-0.5 rounded bg-muted font-mono text-[10px] mx-0.5">2</kbd>
   348           <kbd className="px-1 py-0.5 rounded bg-muted font-mono text-[10px]">3</kbd> pour sélectionner un slot
   349         </div>
   350       )}
   351     </div>
   352   );
   353 };
   354 
   355 export default HandSelector;

     2 // Philosophie : NE PAS se précipiter à effacer une seule ligne.

    56 /** Applique un placement et efface les lignes/cols complètes. Retourne la nouvelle grille + combos. */
    57 function applyAndClear(
    58   grid: boolean[][],
    59   shape: number[][],
    60   row: number,
    61   col: number
    62 ): { grid: boolean[][]; totalClears: number; linesCleared: number; colsCleared: number } {
    63   const g = grid.map(r => [...r]);
    64   for (const [dr, dc] of shape) g[row + dr][col + dc] = true;
    65 
    66   let linesCleared = 0;
    67   let colsCleared = 0;
    68   for (let r = 0; r < GRID_SIZE; r++) {
    69     if (g[r].every(Boolean)) {
    70       for (let c = 0; c < GRID_SIZE; c++) g[r][c] = false;
    71       linesCleared++;
    72     }
    73   }
    74   for (let c = 0; c < GRID_SIZE; c++) {
    75     if (g.every(r => r[c])) {
    76       for (let r = 0; r < GRID_SIZE; r++) g[r][c] = false;
    77       colsCleared++;
    78     }
    79   }
    80   return { grid: g, totalClears: linesCleared + colsCleared, linesCleared, colsCleared };
    81 }
    82 
    83 /** Détecte les lignes/cols effacées AVANT clearance (pour construire les sets d'explosion). */
    84 function getClears(
    85   grid: boolean[][],
    86   shape: number[][],
    87   row: number,
    88   col: number
    89 ): { clearedLines: number[]; clearedCols: number[] } {
    90   const g = grid.map(r => [...r]);
    91   for (const [dr, dc] of shape) g[row + dr][col + dc] = true;
    92   const clearedLines: number[] = [];
    93   const clearedCols: number[] = [];
    94   for (let r = 0; r < GRID_SIZE; r++) if (g[r].every(Boolean)) clearedLines.push(r);
    95   for (let c = 0; c < GRID_SIZE; c++) if (g.every(r => r[c])) clearedCols.push(c);
    96   return { clearedLines, clearedCols };
    97 }
    98 
    99 // ─── Heuristiques de qualité de grille ────────────────────────────────────────
   100 
   101 /**
   102  * Compte les trous isolés (cases vides très encerclées).
   103  * Pénalise fortement les configurations fragmentées.
   104  */
   105 function countHoles(grid: boolean[][]): number {
   106   let holes = 0;
   107   for (let r = 0; r < GRID_SIZE; r++) {
   108     for (let c = 0; c < GRID_SIZE; c++) {
   109       if (grid[r][c]) continue;
   110       const blocked = [
   111         r === 0 || grid[r - 1][c],
   112         r === GRID_SIZE - 1 || grid[r + 1][c],
   113         c === 0 || grid[r][c - 1],
   114         c === GRID_SIZE - 1 || grid[r][c + 1],
   115       ].filter(Boolean).length;
   116       if (blocked >= 3) holes += 2;
   117       else if (blocked === 2) holes += 1;
   118     }
   119   }
   120   return holes;
   121 }
   122 
   123 /**
   124  * Compte les régions vides connectées (flood-fill).
   125  * 1 seule grande région = parfait. Plusieurs petites = mauvais.
   126  */
   127 function countVoidRegions(grid: boolean[][]): number {
   128   const visited = Array.from({ length: GRID_SIZE }, () => new Array(GRID_SIZE).fill(false));
   129   let regions = 0;
   130   const fill = (sr: number, sc: number) => {
   131     const stack = [[sr, sc]];
   132     while (stack.length) {
   133       const [r, c] = stack.pop()!;
   134       if (r < 0 || r >= GRID_SIZE || c < 0 || c >= GRID_SIZE) continue;
   135       if (visited[r][c] || grid[r][c]) continue;
   136       visited[r][c] = true;
   137       stack.push([r - 1, c], [r + 1, c], [r, c - 1], [r, c + 1]);
   138     }
   139   };
   140   for (let r = 0; r < GRID_SIZE; r++) {
   141     for (let c = 0; c < GRID_SIZE; c++) {
   142       if (!grid[r][c] && !visited[r][c]) { regions++; fill(r, c); }
   143     }
   144   }
   145   return regions;
   146 }
   147 
   148 /**
   149  * Score des lignes/cols quasi-complètes — CŒUR de la stratégie setup.
   150  * Plus une ligne est proche de 8/8, plus elle vaut cher.
   151  * Bonus si PLUSIEURS lignes/cols sont simultanément quasi-complètes (potentiel multi-destroy).
   152  */
   153 function setupScore(grid: boolean[][]): { score: number; nearCompleteCount: number } {
   154   let score = 0;
   155   let nearCompleteCount = 0; // lignes/cols à 6+ cases remplies
   156 
   157   for (let r = 0; r < GRID_SIZE; r++) {
   158     const filled = grid[r].filter(Boolean).length;
   159     score += NEAR_COMPLETE_WEIGHT[filled] ?? 0;
   160     if (filled >= 6) nearCompleteCount++;
   161   }
   162   for (let c = 0; c < GRID_SIZE; c++) {
   163     const filled = grid.filter(row => row[c]).length;
   164     score += NEAR_COMPLETE_WEIGHT[filled] ?? 0;
   165     if (filled >= 6) nearCompleteCount++;
   166   }
   167 
   168   // Bonus exponentiel si plusieurs lignes/cols quasi-complètes simultanément
   169   // (potentiel de tout effacer avec UN seul prochain bloc bien placé)
   170   if (nearCompleteCount >= 4) score += nearCompleteCount * 20;
   171   else if (nearCompleteCount >= 2) score += nearCompleteCount * 8;
   172 
   173   return { score, nearCompleteCount };
   174 }
   175 
   176 /**
   177  * Évaluation heuristique complète d'un état de grille.
   178  * Intègre: setup (lignes quasi-complètes), fragmentation, trous, densité.
   179  */
   180 function evaluateGrid(grid: boolean[][]): number {
   181   const { score: setup } = setupScore(grid);
   182   const holes = countHoles(grid);
   183   const regions = countVoidRegions(grid);
   184   const totalFilled = grid.flat().filter(Boolean).length;
   185   const density = totalFilled / 64;
   186   // Légère préférence pour la moitié inférieure de remplissage (plus d'options)
   187   const densityPenalty = density > 0.6 ? (density - 0.6) * 30 : 0;
   188 
   189   return (
   190     setup
   191     - holes * HOLE_PENALTY
   192     - (regions - 1) * FRAGMENTATION_PENALTY
   193     - densityPenalty
   194   );
   195 }
   196 
   197 // ─── Échantillonnage représentatif du catalogue ──────────────────────────────
   198 
   199 /**
   200  * Sélectionne un sous-ensemble représentatif et diversifié du catalogue
   201  * pour simuler les blocs futurs inconnus du joueur.
   202  * Couvre les différentes tailles et formes du catalogue.
   203  */
   204 function sampleCatalog(): typeof BLOCK_CATALOG {
   205   if (BLOCK_CATALOG.length <= CATALOG_SAMPLE_SIZE) return BLOCK_CATALOG;
   206 
   207   // Grouper par taille
   208   const bySize: Record<number, typeof BLOCK_CATALOG> = {};
   209   for (const def of BLOCK_CATALOG) {
   210     if (!bySize[def.size]) bySize[def.size] = [];
   211     bySize[def.size].push(def);
   212   }
   213 
   214   const sample: typeof BLOCK_CATALOG = [];
   215   const sizes = Object.keys(bySize).map(Number).sort();
   216 
   217   // Proportionnel à la représentation dans le catalogue
   218   for (const size of sizes) {
   219     const group = bySize[size];
   220     const proportion = Math.max(1, Math.round((group.length / BLOCK_CATALOG.length) * CATALOG_SAMPLE_SIZE));
   221     // Prendre des éléments espacés régulièrement dans le groupe
   222     const step = Math.max(1, Math.floor(group.length / proportion));
   223     for (let i = 0; i < group.length && sample.length < CATALOG_SAMPLE_SIZE; i += step) {
   224       sample.push(group[i]);
   225     }
   226   }
   227 
   228   return sample;
   229 }
   230 
   231 // Cache de l'échantillon (stable pendant la session)
   232 let _catalogSample: typeof BLOCK_CATALOG | null = null;
   233 function getCatalogSample(): typeof BLOCK_CATALOG {
   234   if (!_catalogSample) _catalogSample = sampleCatalog();
   235   return _catalogSample;
   236 }
   237 
   238 // ─── Look-ahead futur via catalogue ──────────────────────────────────────────
   239 
   240 /**
   241  * Estime l'espérance de gain futur en testant des blocs représentatifs du catalogue
   242  * sur la grille résultante d'un placement candidat.
   243  *
   244  * Pour chaque bloc futur échantillonné :
   245  *   - Trouve son MEILLEUR placement possible
   246  *   - Calcule le combo immédiat + la qualité de grille résultante
   247  *
   248  * Retourne la moyenne (espérance) sur tous les blocs testés.
   249  */
   250 function futurePotential(
   251   gridAfter: boolean[][],
   252   color: string
   253 ): { expectedValue: number; bestFutureClears: number } {
   254   const sample = getCatalogSample();
   255   let totalScore = 0;
   256   let samplesUsed = 0;
   257   let bestFutureClears = 0;
   258 
   259   for (const def of sample) {
   260     const transforms = getUniqueTransforms(def, color);
   261     let bestForThisBlock = -Infinity;
   262     let bestClearsForThisBlock = 0;
   263 
   264     for (const t of transforms) {
   265       const shape = getInstanceShape(t);
   266       for (let r = 0; r < GRID_SIZE; r++) {
   267         for (let c = 0; c < GRID_SIZE; c++) {
   268           if (!canPlace(gridAfter, shape, r, c)) continue;
   269           const { grid: g2, totalClears, linesCleared, colsCleared } =
   270             applyAndClear(gridAfter, shape, r, c);
   271 
   272           // Score de ce futur placement
   273           const immScore = comboBonus(totalClears)
   274             + (linesCleared > 0 && colsCleared > 0 ? CROSS_CLEAR_BONUS : 0);
   275           const stateScore = evaluateGrid(g2);
   276           const total = immScore + stateScore * 0.5;
   277 
   278           if (total > bestForThisBlock) {
   279             bestForThisBlock = total;
   280             bestClearsForThisBlock = totalClears;
   281           }
   282         }
   283       }
   284     }
   285 
   286     if (bestForThisBlock > -Infinity) {
   287       totalScore += bestForThisBlock;
   288       samplesUsed++;
   289       if (bestClearsForThisBlock > bestFutureClears)
   290         bestFutureClears = bestClearsForThisBlock;
   291     }
   292   }
   293 
   294   return {
   295     expectedValue: samplesUsed > 0 ? totalScore / samplesUsed : 0,
   296     bestFutureClears,
   297   };
   298 }
   299 
   300 // ─── Évaluation d'un placement candidat ─────────────────────────────────────
   301 
   302 interface CandidateScore {
   303   immediateScore: number;
   304   setupScore_: number;
   305   futureScore: number;
   306   totalScore: number;
   307   linesCleared: number;
   308   colsCleared: number;
   309   clearedLines: number[];
   310   clearedCols: number[];
   311   nearCompleteCount: number;
   312   bestFutureClears: number;
   313 }
   314 
   315 /**
   316  * Score un placement candidat en tenant compte :
   317  * - Du combo immédiat (non-linéaire)
   318  * - Du setup futur (lignes quasi-complètes après placement)
   319  * - De l'espérance future via catalogue
   320  * - De la zone réservée boss (pénalité si empiètement)
   321  * - De la mémoire contextuelle (bonus si continuité stratégique)
   322  */
   323 function scoreCandidate(
   324   grid: boolean[][],
   325   shape: number[][],
   326   row: number,
   327   col: number,
   328   color: string,
   329   reservedCells: Set<string> = new Set(),
   330   memory: ClearMemory[] = [],
   331   isBossBlock = false
   332 ): CandidateScore {
   333   const { clearedLines, clearedCols } = getClears(grid, shape, row, col);
   334   const { grid: gridAfter, linesCleared, colsCleared } =
   335     applyAndClear(grid, shape, row, col);
   336 
   337   const totalClears = linesCleared + colsCleared;
   338   const hasCross = linesCleared > 0 && colsCleared > 0;
   339 
   340   // ① Score immédiat (combo non-linéaire)
   341   const immediateScore =
   342     comboBonus(totalClears)
   343     + (hasCross ? CROSS_CLEAR_BONUS : 0);
   344 
   345   // ② Score setup
   346   const { score: ss, nearCompleteCount } = setupScore(gridAfter);
   347   const holes = countHoles(gridAfter);
   348   const regions = countVoidRegions(gridAfter);
   349   const density = gridAfter.flat().filter(Boolean).length / 64;
   350   const densityPenalty = density > 0.6 ? (density - 0.6) * 30 : 0;
   351   const setupScore_ = ss - holes * HOLE_PENALTY - (regions - 1) * FRAGMENTATION_PENALTY - densityPenalty;
   352 
   353   // ③ Potentiel futur via catalogue
   354   const { expectedValue: futureScore, bestFutureClears } = futurePotential(gridAfter, color);
   355 
   356   // ④ Pénalité zone réservée boss (uniquement pour les blocs NON-boss)
   357   let reservedPenalty = 0;
   358   if (!isBossBlock && reservedCells.size > 0) {
   359     const overlap = shape.filter(([dr, dc]) => reservedCells.has(`${row + dr},${col + dc}`)).length;
   360     if (overlap > 0) reservedPenalty = RESERVED_ZONE_PENALTY * overlap;
   361   }
   362 
   363   // ⑤ Bonus mémoire contextuelle
   364   // Si on complète une ligne/col qui a été active récemment → on continue la bonne direction
   365   let memoryBonus = 0;
   366   if (memory.length > 0) {
   367     const recentLines = new Set(memory.flatMap(m => m.lines));
   368     const recentCols = new Set(memory.flatMap(m => m.cols));
   369     // Lignes/cols qui seraient effacées ET qui continuent une direction active
   370     for (const l of clearedLines) if (recentLines.has(l)) memoryBonus += MEMORY_BONUS;
   371     for (const c of clearedCols) if (recentCols.has(c)) memoryBonus += MEMORY_BONUS;
   372     // Bonus plus faible si on approche d'une ligne/col active (sans l'effacer)
   373     for (let r = 0; r < GRID_SIZE; r++) {
   374       if (recentLines.has(r)) {
   375         const filledAfter = gridAfter[r].filter(Boolean).length;
   376         if (filledAfter >= 6) memoryBonus += 8;
   377       }
   378     }
   379     for (let c = 0; c < GRID_SIZE; c++) {
   380       if (recentCols.has(c)) {
   381         const filledAfter = gridAfter.filter(r2 => r2[c]).length;
   382         if (filledAfter >= 6) memoryBonus += 8;
   383       }
   384     }
   385   }
   386 
   387   const totalScore =
   388     immediateScore * 1.0
   389     + setupScore_ * 2.5
   390     + futureScore * FUTURE_WEIGHT
   391     - reservedPenalty
   392     + memoryBonus;
   393 
   394   return {
   395     immediateScore,
   396     setupScore_,
   397     futureScore,
   398     totalScore,
   399     linesCleared,
   400     colsCleared,
   401     clearedLines,
   402     clearedCols,
   403     nearCompleteCount,
   404     bestFutureClears,
   405   };
   406 }
   407 
   408 // ─── Génération des suggestions ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   409 
   410 function suggestionsForBlock(
   411   block: BlockInstance,
   412   grid: boolean[][],
   413   maxSuggestions = 5,
   414   reservedCells: Set<string> = new Set(),
   415   memory: ClearMemory[] = [],
   416   isBossBlock = false
   417 ): Suggestion[] {
   418   const candidates: Suggestion[] = [];
   419   const transforms = getUniqueTransforms(block.definition, block.color);
   420 
   421   for (const transform of transforms) {
   422     const shape = getInstanceShape(transform);
   423 
   424     for (let row = 0; row < GRID_SIZE; row++) {
   425       for (let col = 0; col < GRID_SIZE; col++) {
   426         if (!canPlace(grid, shape, row, col)) continue;
   427 
   428         const s = scoreCandidate(grid, shape, row, col, block.color, reservedCells, memory, isBossBlock);
   429 
   430         // Étiquette lisible du potentiel combo futur
   431         let comboLabel: string | undefined;
   432         const totalFutureLines = s.nearCompleteCount + s.bestFutureClears;
   433         if (s.linesCleared + s.colsCleared >= 3) {
   434           comboLabel = `💥 ${s.linesCleared + s.colsCleared} lignes/cols !`;
   435         } else if (s.linesCleared > 0 && s.colsCleared > 0) {
   436           comboLabel = `⚡ Croix (×${s.linesCleared + s.colsCleared})`;
   437         } else if (s.linesCleared + s.colsCleared === 2) {
   438           comboLabel = `⚡ Double`;
   439         } else if (s.nearCompleteCount >= 4) {
   440           comboLabel = `🎯 Setup ×${s.nearCompleteCount}`;
   441         } else if (s.nearCompleteCount >= 2) {
   442           comboLabel = `🎯 Setup ×${s.nearCompleteCount}`;
   443         } else if (s.bestFutureClears >= 2) {
   444           comboLabel = `🔮 Futur ×${s.bestFutureClears}`;
   445         } else if (totalFutureLines >= 3) {
   446           comboLabel = `📐 ${totalFutureLines} prêts`;
   447         }
   448 
   449         candidates.push({
   450           id: `${transform.definition.id}-${transform.rotation}-${transform.flipped}-${row}-${col}`,
   451           blockInstance: transform,
   452           position: { row, col },
   453           score: Math.round(s.totalScore),
   454           linesCleared: s.linesCleared,
   455           colsCleared: s.colsCleared,
   456           cellsFreed: (s.linesCleared + s.colsCleared) * GRID_SIZE,
   457           affectedCells: shape.map(([dr, dc]) => [row + dr, col + dc] as [number, number]),
   458           clearedLines: s.clearedLines,
   459           clearedCols: s.clearedCols,
   460           futureComboLines: s.nearCompleteCount,
   461           comboLabel,
   462         });
   463       }
   464     }
   465   }
   466 
   467   return candidates
   468     .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)
   469     .slice(0, maxSuggestions);
   470 }
   471 
   472 // ─── Identification du Boss ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
   473 
   474 /**
   475  * Identifie le slot "boss" : le bloc le plus grand de la main.
   476  * Par convention du jeu, c'est toujours le slot du milieu (index 1).
   477  * On vérifie quand même par taille pour être robuste.
   478  */
   479 export function findBossSlot(hand: Array<BlockInstance | null>): number {
   480   let maxSize = -1;
   481   let bossIdx = 1; // par défaut : milieu
   482   hand.forEach((block, idx) => {
   483     if (block && block.definition.size > maxSize) {
   484       maxSize = block.definition.size;
   485       bossIdx = idx;
   486     }
   487   });
   488   return bossIdx;
   489 }
   490 
   491 /**
   492  * Calcule la meilleure zone réservée pour le bloc boss sur la grille actuelle.
   493  * Cherche la position qui maximise le potentiel de combo futur pour le boss.
   494  * Retourne null si aucune position valide n'existe.
   495  */
   496 export function computeBossReservation(
   497   grid: Grid,
   498   bossBlock: BlockInstance,
   499   bossSlot: number,
   500   memory: ClearMemory[] = []
   501 ): BossReservation | null {
   502   const boolGrid = gridToBool(grid);
   503   const transforms = getUniqueTransforms(bossBlock.definition, bossBlock.color);
   504 
   505   let bestScore = -Infinity;
   506   let bestResult: BossReservation | null = null;
   507 
   508   for (const transform of transforms) {
   509     const shape = getInstanceShape(transform);
   510     for (let row = 0; row < GRID_SIZE; row++) {
   511       for (let col = 0; col < GRID_SIZE; col++) {
   512         if (!canPlace(boolGrid, shape, row, col)) continue;
   513         // Pour le boss, on évalue sans pénalité de zone réservée (c'est lui le boss!)
   514         const s = scoreCandidate(boolGrid, shape, row, col, bossBlock.color, new Set(), memory, true);
   515         if (s.totalScore > bestScore) {
   516           bestScore = s.totalScore;
   517           bestResult = {
   518             cells: shape.map(([dr, dc]) => [row + dr, col + dc] as [number, number]),
   519             row,
   520             col,
   521             bossBlock: transform,
   522             bossSlot,
   523           };
   524         }
   525       }
   526     }
   527   }
   528 
   529   return bestResult;
   530 }
   531 
   532 /**
   533  * Convertit une BossReservation en Set<string> de clés "row,col" pour comparaison rapide.
   534  */
   535 export function reservationToCellSet(reservation: BossReservation | null): Set<string> {
   536   if (!reservation) return new Set();
   537   return new Set(reservation.cells.map(([r, c]) => `${r},${c}`));
   538 }

   567 /**
   568  * Vérifie si un bloc peut être placé quelque part sur la grille.
   569  */
   570 export function canBlockBePlaced(grid: Grid, block: BlockInstance): boolean {
   571   const boolGrid = gridToBool(grid);
   572   const transforms = getUniqueTransforms(block.definition, block.color);
   573   for (const transform of transforms) {
   574     const shape = getInstanceShape(transform);
   575     for (let row = 0; row < GRID_SIZE; row++) {
   576       for (let col = 0; col < GRID_SIZE; col++) {
   577         if (canPlace(boolGrid, shape, row, col)) return true;
   578       }
   579     }
   580   }
   581   return false;
   582 }
   583 
   584 /**
   585  * Suggère automatiquement 3 nouveaux blocs pour recharger la main.
   586  * GARANTIT que le slot 1 (milieu) reçoit le plus grand bloc (le nouveau boss).
   587  * Slots 0 et 2 reçoivent des blocs plus petits compatibles.
   588  */
   589 export function suggestNextBlocks(
   590   grid: Grid,
   591   colors: string[],
   592   count = 3
   593 ): BlockInstance[] {
   594   const boolGrid = gridToBool(grid);
   595 
   596   // Scorer chaque bloc du catalogue sur son MEILLEUR placement possible
   597   const scored = BLOCK_CATALOG.map((def, idx) => {
   598     const color = colors[idx % colors.length] || colors[0];
   599     const transforms = getUniqueTransforms(def, color);
   600 
   601     let bestTotalScore = -Infinity;
   602     let bestSetup = 0;
   603 
   604     for (const instance of transforms) {
   605       const shape = getInstanceShape(instance);
   606       for (let row = 0; row < GRID_SIZE; row++) {
   607         for (let col = 0; col < GRID_SIZE; col++) {
   608           if (!canPlace(boolGrid, shape, row, col)) continue;
   609           const s = scoreCandidate(boolGrid, shape, row, col, color);
   610           if (s.totalScore > bestTotalScore) {
   611             bestTotalScore = s.totalScore;
   612             bestSetup = s.nearCompleteCount;
   613           }
   614         }
   615       }
   616     }
   617 
   618     if (bestTotalScore === -Infinity) return { def, color, totalScore: -1000, setup: 0 };
   619     return { def, color, totalScore: bestTotalScore + bestSetup * 5, setup: bestSetup };
   620   });
   621 
   622   scored.sort((a, b) => b.totalScore - a.totalScore);
   623 
   624   // Sélectionner `count` blocs diversifiés (taille et série variées)
   625   const selected: BlockInstance[] = [];
   626   const usedSeries = new Set<string>();
   627   const sizes: number[] = [];
   628 
   629   for (const { def, color } of scored) {
   630     if (selected.length >= count) break;
   631     const seriesSaturated = usedSeries.has(def.series) && selected.length < count - 1;
   632     const sizeSaturated = sizes.filter(s => s === def.size).length >= 2;
   633     if (seriesSaturated || sizeSaturated) continue;
   634     usedSeries.add(def.series);
   635     sizes.push(def.size);
   636     selected.push({ definition: def, rotation: 0, flipped: false, color });
   637   }
   638 
   639   // Compléter si pas assez
   640   if (selected.length < count) {
   641     for (const { def, color } of scored) {
   642       if (selected.length >= count) break;
   643       if (!selected.some(s => s.definition.id === def.id)) {
   644         selected.push({ definition: def, rotation: 0, flipped: false, color });
   645       }
   646     }
   647   }
   648 
   649   // ── RÈGLE DU BOSS ──
   650   // Garantir que le slot 1 (milieu) est toujours le plus GRAND bloc.
   651   // Trier selected par taille : [petit, grand, moyen] → mettre le plus grand au centre.
   652   if (selected.length === 3) {
   653     selected.sort((a, b) => a.definition.size - b.definition.size);
   654     // Après tri ascendant : [0]=petit, [1]=moyen, [2]=grand
   655     // On veut : [0]=petit, [1]=grand(boss), [2]=moyen
   656     const [small, medium, large] = selected;
   657     return [small, large, medium];
   658   }
   659 
   660   return selected;
   661 }
   662 
   663 /**
   664  * Suggère un seul nouveau bloc pour un slot non-boss (shuffle).
   665  * Compatible avec l'état de la grille et ne bloque pas la zone réservée du boss.
   666  */
   667 export function suggestOneBlock(
   668   grid: Grid,
   669   colors: string[],
   670   excludeIds: string[] = [],
   671   bossReservation: BossReservation | null = null,
   672   memory: ClearMemory[] = []
   673 ): BlockInstance | null {
   674   const boolGrid = gridToBool(grid);
   675   const reservedCells = reservationToCellSet(bossReservation);
   676 
   677   const scored = BLOCK_CATALOG
   678     .filter(def => !excludeIds.includes(def.id))
   679     .map((def, idx) => {
   680       const color = colors[idx % colors.length] || colors[0];
   681       const transforms = getUniqueTransforms(def, color);
   682 
   683       let bestScore = -Infinity;
   684       for (const instance of transforms) {
   685         const shape = getInstanceShape(instance);
   686         for (let row = 0; row < GRID_SIZE; row++) {
   687           for (let col = 0; col < GRID_SIZE; col++) {
   688             if (!canPlace(boolGrid, shape, row, col)) continue;
   689             const s = scoreCandidate(boolGrid, shape, row, col, color, reservedCells, memory, false);
   690             if (s.totalScore > bestScore) bestScore = s.totalScore;
   691           }
   692         }
   693       }
   694 
   695       if (bestScore === -Infinity) return null;
   696       return { def, color, score: bestScore };
   697     })
   698     .filter((x): x is { def: typeof BLOCK_CATALOG[0]; color: string; score: number } => x !== null);
   699 
   700   scored.sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);


</observation>

    65   // Recalcule le boss + sa zone réservée à chaque changement de main ou grille
    66   const recomputeBoss = useCallback(
    67     (currentGrid: Grid, currentHand: Array<BlockInstance | null>, currentMemory: ClearMemory[]) => {
    68       const newBossSlot = findBossSlot(currentHand);
    69       setBossSlot(newBossSlot);

    77     },
    78     []
    79   );

    81   // Recalculer le boss quand la main change
    82   useEffect(() => {
    83     recomputeBoss(grid, hand, clearMemory);
    84     // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
    85   }, [hand]);

    87   const occupiedCount = grid.flat().filter(c => c.occupied).length;

    89   // ── Peinture manuelle ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    90   const handleCellClick = useCallback(
    91     (row: number, col: number) => {
    92       if (kbSlot !== null) return;
    93       setGrid(prev => {
    94         const next = prev.map(r => r.map(c => ({ ...c })));
    95         if (paintMode === 'erase') {
    96           next[row][col] = { occupied: false, color: null };

    99           if (cell.occupied && cell.color === selectedColor) {
   100             next[row][col] = { occupied: false, color: null };
   101           } else {
   102             next[row][col] = { occupied: true, color: selectedColor };
   103           }
   104         }
   105         return next;
   106       });
   107       if (hasAnalyzed) { setSuggestions({}); setHasAnalyzed(false); }

   112   const handleSlotChange = useCallback(
   113     (slot: 0 | 1 | 2, block: BlockInstance | null) => {
   114       setHand(prev => {

   219   // ── Recharger la main si tous les slots sont vides ──────────────────────
   220   const refillHandIfEmpty = useCallback(
   221     (updatedHand: Array<BlockInstance | null>, currentGrid: Grid, currentMemory: ClearMemory[]): Array<BlockInstance | null> => {
   222       const allEmpty = updatedHand.every(b => b === null);
   223       if (!allEmpty) return updatedHand;

   238   // ── Logique centrale : placer un bloc + effacer lignes/cols + score ───────
   239   const triggerPlacementResult = useCallback(
   240     (
   241       newGrid: Grid,
   242       result: { clearedLines: number[]; clearedCols: number[]; scoreGained: number; cellsFreed: number },
   243       newHand: Array<BlockInstance | null> | null,

   245     ) => {
   246       const { clearedLines, clearedCols, scoreGained, cellsFreed } = result;
   247       const combos = clearedLines.length + clearedCols.length;
   248 
   249       const toExplode = new Set<string>();
   250       for (const r of clearedLines) {
   251         for (let c = 0; c < GRID_SIZE; c++) toExplode.add(`${r},${c}`);
   252       }
   253       for (const col of clearedCols) {
   254         for (let r = 0; r < GRID_SIZE; r++) toExplode.add(`${r},${col}`);
   255       }
   256 
   257       setGrid(newGrid);
   258 
   259       if (toExplode.size > 0) {
   260         setExplodingCells(toExplode);
   261         if (explodeTimerRef.current) clearTimeout(explodeTimerRef.current);
   262         explodeTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
   263           setExplodingCells(new Set());
   264           if (newHand) {
   265             setHand(newHand);
   266           }
   267           // Recalculer boss après effacement + nouvelle main
   268           recomputeBoss(newGrid, newHand ?? [], newMemory);
   269           setSuggestions({});
   270           setHasAnalyzed(false);
   271         }, 500);
   272       } else {
   273         if (newHand) setHand(newHand);
   274         recomputeBoss(newGrid, newHand ?? [], newMemory);
   275         setSuggestions({});
   276         setHasAnalyzed(false);
   277       }
   278 
   279       if (scoreGained > 0) {
   280         setScore(prev => prev + scoreGained);

   283         popupKeyRef.current += 1;
   284         setScorePopup({ value: scoreGained, key: popupKeyRef.current });
   285         setTimeout(() => setScorePopup(null), 1100);
   286         const comboMsg = combos > 1 ? ` (×${combos} combo !)` : '';
   287         toast.success(`🎉 ${cellsFreed} cases libérées${comboMsg}`, {
   288           description: `+${scoreGained} points`,
   289           duration: 2000,
   290         });
   291       }
   292     },
   293     [recomputeBoss]
   294   );
   295 
   296   // Construit la nouvelle mémoire après un placement
   297   const buildNewMemory = useCallback(
   298     (clearedLines: number[], clearedCols: number[]): ClearMemory[] => {
   299       if (clearedLines.length === 0 && clearedCols.length === 0) return clearMemory;
   300       turnCountRef.current += 1;
   301       const newEntry: ClearMemory = {
   302         lines: clearedLines,
   303         cols: clearedCols,
   304         turn: turnCountRef.current,

   310       return trimmed;
   311     },
   312     [clearMemory]

   314 
   315   // ── Appliquer une suggestion ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   316   const handleApplySuggestion = useCallback((suggestion: Suggestion) => {
   317     const shape = getInstanceShape(suggestion.blockInstance);
   318     const result = applyPlacementWithClears(
   319       grid,

   329     const updatedHand = [...hand] as Array<BlockInstance | null>;
   330     if (slotIndex >= 0) updatedHand[slotIndex] = null;
   331     const newMemory = buildNewMemory(result.clearedLines, result.clearedCols);
   332     const finalHand = refillHandIfEmpty(updatedHand, result.newGrid, newMemory);
   333     triggerPlacementResult(result.newGrid, result, finalHand, newMemory);
   334     setHoveredSuggestion(null);
   335   }, [grid, hand, suggestions, refillHandIfEmpty, triggerPlacementResult, buildNewMemory]);
   336 
   337   // ── Placer un bloc (drag, clavier) ───────────────────────────────────────
   338   const placeBlock = useCallback(
   339     (block: BlockInstance, slotIndex: number, anchorRow: number, anchorCol: number): boolean => {
   340       const shape = getInstanceShape(block);
   341       const boolGrid = gridToBool(grid);
   342       if (!canPlace(boolGrid, shape, anchorRow, anchorCol)) return false;
   343       const result = applyPlacementWithClears(grid, shape, anchorRow, anchorCol, block.color);
   344       const updatedHand = [...hand] as Array<BlockInstance | null>;
   345       if (slotIndex >= 0) updatedHand[slotIndex] = null;
   346       const newMemory = buildNewMemory(result.clearedLines, result.clearedCols);
   347       const finalHand = refillHandIfEmpty(updatedHand, result.newGrid, newMemory);
   348       triggerPlacementResult(result.newGrid, result, finalHand, newMemory);
   349       return true;
   350     },
   351     [grid, hand, refillHandIfEmpty, triggerPlacementResult, buildNewMemory]
   352   );
   353 
   354   // ── Drop depuis la Main ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
   355   const handleBlockDropped = useCallback(
   356     (block: BlockInstance, slotIndex: number, row: number, col: number) => {
   357       const ok = placeBlock(block, slotIndex, row, col);

   363         });
   364       }
   365     },
   366     [placeBlock]
   367   );
   368 
   369   // ── Mode clavier ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   370   const handleKeyDown = useCallback(
   371     (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
   372       if (e.target instanceof HTMLInputElement || e.target instanceof HTMLTextAreaElement) return;
   373       if (e.key === '1' && hand[0]) { setKbSlot(0); e.preventDefault(); }
   374       else if (e.key === '2' && hand[1]) { setKbSlot(1); e.preventDefault(); }
   375       else if (e.key === '3' && hand[2]) { setKbSlot(2); e.preventDefault(); }
   376       else if (e.key === 'Escape') { setKbSlot(null); }
   377     },
   378     [hand]
   379   );
   380 
   381   const handleKeyboardPlace = useCallback(
   382     (row: number, col: number) => {
   383       if (kbSlot === null) return;
   384       const block = hand[kbSlot];
   385       if (!block) return;
   386       const ok = placeBlock(block, kbSlot, row, col);
   387       if (ok) {
   388         toast.success(`Bloc ${block.definition.name} placé !`, {
   389           description: `Clavier — Ligne ${row + 1}, colonne ${col + 1}`,
   390         });
   391         setKbSlot(null);
   392       } else {
   393         toast.error('Placement invalide', { description: 'Choisissez une position libre.' });
   394       }
   395     },
   396     [kbSlot, hand, placeBlock]
   397   );
   398 
   399   // Cellules réservées pour l'overlay boss
   400   const reservedZoneCells = reservationToCellSet(bossReservation);
   401   const bossBlock = hand[bossSlot];
   402   const bossColor = bossBlock?.color ?? theme.accentColor;
   403

```
// ─── Cache IA — Apprentissage automatisé ─────────────────────────────────────
// Évite de recalculer ce qu'on connaît déjà.
// Clé de cache = empreinte compacte de la grille + identifiants des blocs.
// Le cache survit aux re-renders mais est réinitialisé entre les sessions (mémoire).

export interface CacheStats {
  hits: number;
  misses: number;
  entries: number;
  hitRate: number; // 0-1
}

// Taille maximale du cache (entrées LRU)
const MAX_CACHE_SIZE = 256;

// Structure interne d'une entrée de cache
interface CacheEntry<T> {
  value: T;
  timestamp: number;
  hits: number;
}

class LRUCache<T> {
  private map = new Map<string, CacheEntry<T>>();
  private stats = { hits: 0, misses: 0 };

  get(key: string): T | undefined {
    const entry = this.map.get(key);
    if (!entry) {
      this.stats.misses++;
      return undefined;
    }
    // Refresh LRU order
    this.map.delete(key);
    entry.hits++;
    this.map.set(key, entry);
    this.stats.hits++;
    return entry.value;
  }

  set(key: string, value: T): void {
    if (this.map.has(key)) this.map.delete(key);
    else if (this.map.size >= MAX_CACHE_SIZE) {
      // Éviction de l'entrée la plus ancienne (premier élément de la Map)
      const firstKey = this.map.keys().next().value;
      if (firstKey !== undefined) this.map.delete(firstKey);
    }
    this.map.set(key, { value, timestamp: Date.now(), hits: 0 });
  }

  clear(): void {
    this.map.clear();
    this.stats = { hits: 0, misses: 0 };
  }

  getStats(): CacheStats {
    const total = this.stats.hits + this.stats.misses;
    return {
      hits: this.stats.hits,
      misses: this.stats.misses,
      entries: this.map.size,
      hitRate: total > 0 ? this.stats.hits / total : 0,
    };
  }

  get size(): number { return this.map.size; }
}

// ─── Instances globales ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────

/** Cache pour computeBossReservation */
export const bossCache = new LRUCache<unknown>();

/** Cache pour generateSuggestions */
export const suggestionsCache = new LRUCache<unknown>();

/** Cache pour suggestNextBlocks */
export const nextBlocksCache = new LRUCache<unknown>();

/** Cache pour canBlockBePlaced (résultats par bloc+grille) */
export const placabilityCache = new LRUCache<boolean>();

// ─── Fonctions d'empreinte ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

/**
 * Génère une empreinte compacte et déterministe d'une grille booléenne.
 * Encode chaque ligne en valeur numérique (8 bits = 1 octet).
 * Beaucoup plus rapide que JSON.stringify.
 */
export function gridFingerprint(grid: boolean[][]): string {
  // Chaque ligne → un nombre 0-255 (8 cases = 8 bits)
  return grid.map(row =>
    row.reduce((acc, cell, i) => acc | (cell ? 1 << i : 0), 0).toString(36)
  ).join(',');
}

/**
 * Empreinte d'un bloc : id + rotation + flip.
 */
export function blockFingerprint(blockId: string, rotation: number, flipped: boolean, color: string): string {
  return `${blockId}:${rotation}:${flipped ? 1 : 0}:${color}`;
}

/**
 * Clé composite pour une main complète + grille + mémoire résumée.
 */
export function handGridKey(
  gridFp: string,
  handIds: Array<string | null>,
  memoryHash: string
): string {
  return `${gridFp}|${handIds.join(',')}|${memoryHash}`;
}

/**
 * Résume la mémoire contextuelle en une chaîne compacte.
 */
export function memoryFingerprint(memory: Array<{ lines: number[]; cols: number[]; turn: number }>): string {
  if (memory.length === 0) return '';
  return memory.map(m => `${m.lines.join('-')}x${m.cols.join('-')}@${m.turn}`).join(';');
}

// ─── Réinitialisation globale ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

export function clearAllCaches(): void {
  bossCache.clear();
  suggestionsCache.clear();
  nextBlocksCache.clear();
  placabilityCache.clear();
}

export function getAllCacheStats(): { boss: CacheStats; suggestions: CacheStats; nextBlocks: CacheStats; placability: CacheStats; combined: CacheStats } {
  const b = bossCache.getStats();
  const s = suggestionsCache.getStats();
  const n = nextBlocksCache.getStats();
  const p = placabilityCache.getStats();
  const totalHits = b.hits + s.hits + n.hits + p.hits;
  const totalMisses = b.misses + s.misses + n.misses + p.misses;
  const totalEntries = b.entries + s.entries + n.entries + p.entries;
  return {
    boss: b,
    suggestions: s,
    nextBlocks: n,
    placability: p,
    combined: {
      hits: totalHits,
      misses: totalMisses,
      entries: totalEntries,
      hitRate: (totalHits + totalMisses) > 0 ? totalHits / (totalHits + totalMisses) : 0,
    },
  };
}

```

```
// Hook de journal d'activités IA — suivi en temps réel de chaque opération background
import { useState, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';

export type ActivityStatus = 'running' | 'done' | 'cached' | 'error';

export interface ActivityEntry {
  id: string;
  label: string;         // Texte court affiché
  detail?: string;       // Détail optionnel (ex: "depuis cache", "3 suggestions")
  status: ActivityStatus;
  startedAt: number;     // timestamp ms
  durationMs?: number;   // rempli quand status = done|cached|error
}

const MAX_LOG = 8; // garder les N dernières activités visibles

export function useActivityLog() {
  const [entries, setEntries] = useState<ActivityEntry[]>([]);
  const counterRef = useRef(0);

  /** Démarre une activité → retourne son id pour la terminer ensuite */
  const startActivity = useCallback((label: string, detail?: string): string => {
    const id = `act-${++counterRef.current}`;
    const entry: ActivityEntry = {
      id,
      label,
      detail,
      status: 'running',
      startedAt: Date.now(),
    };
    setEntries(prev => {
      const next = [entry, ...prev];
      return next.slice(0, MAX_LOG);
    });
    return id;
  }, []);

  /** Termine une activité avec son statut final */
  const finishActivity = useCallback((
    id: string,
    status: Exclude<ActivityStatus, 'running'>,
    detail?: string
  ) => {
    setEntries(prev =>
      prev.map(e => e.id === id
        ? { ...e, status, detail: detail ?? e.detail, durationMs: Date.now() - e.startedAt }
        : e
      )
    );
  }, []);

  /** Raccourci : enregistre une activité déjà terminée (ex: résultat depuis cache) */
  const logInstant = useCallback((
    label: string,
    status: Exclude<ActivityStatus, 'running'>,
    detail?: string
  ) => {
    const id = `act-${++counterRef.current}`;
    const entry: ActivityEntry = {
      id,
      label,
      detail,
      status,
      startedAt: Date.now(),
      durationMs: 0,
    };
    setEntries(prev => [entry, ...prev].slice(0, MAX_LOG));
  }, []);

  const clearLog = useCallback(() => setEntries([]), []);

  return { entries, startActivity, finishActivity, logInstant, clearLog };
}

```

```
// Panneau de journal d'activités IA — affiche chaque opération background en temps réel
import React from 'react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import type { ActivityEntry, ActivityStatus } from '@/hooks/useActivityLog';
import { Loader2, CheckCircle2, Zap, AlertCircle, Brain } from 'lucide-react';
import type { CacheStats } from '@/lib/aiCache';

interface ActivityPanelProps {
  entries: ActivityEntry[];
  cacheStats?: CacheStats;
  className?: string;
}

function statusIcon(status: ActivityStatus) {
  switch (status) {
    case 'running':
      return <Loader2 className="h-3 w-3 animate-spin text-blue-500 flex-shrink-0" />;
    case 'done':
      return <CheckCircle2 className="h-3 w-3 text-green-500 flex-shrink-0" />;
    case 'cached':
      return <Zap className="h-3 w-3 text-yellow-500 flex-shrink-0" />;
    case 'error':
      return <AlertCircle className="h-3 w-3 text-destructive flex-shrink-0" />;
  }
}

function statusLabel(status: ActivityStatus): string {
  switch (status) {
    case 'running': return 'en cours…';
    case 'done':    return 'terminé';
    case 'cached':  return 'cache ⚡';
    case 'error':   return 'erreur';
  }
}

function statusColor(status: ActivityStatus): string {
  switch (status) {
    case 'running': return 'text-blue-500';
    case 'done':    return 'text-green-600 dark:text-green-400';
    case 'cached':  return 'text-yellow-600 dark:text-yellow-400';
    case 'error':   return 'text-destructive';
  }
}

function durationBadge(entry: ActivityEntry): string | null {
  if (entry.status === 'running') return null;
  if (entry.durationMs === undefined) return null;
  if (entry.durationMs < 1) return entry.status === 'cached' ? '< 1 ms' : null;
  return `${entry.durationMs} ms`;
}

export const ActivityPanel: React.FC<ActivityPanelProps> = ({ entries, cacheStats, className }) => {
  const hasRunning = entries.some(e => e.status === 'running');

  return (
    <div className={cn('flex flex-col gap-1.5', className)}>
      {/* En-tête avec indicateur de cache global */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
          <Brain className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground flex-shrink-0" />
          <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-foreground">Journal IA</span>
          {hasRunning && (
            <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-blue-500 font-medium">
              <Loader2 className="h-2.5 w-2.5 animate-spin" />
              calcul…
            </span>
          )}
        </div>
        {cacheStats && cacheStats.entries > 0 && (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground font-mono shrink-0">
            <Zap className="h-2.5 w-2.5 text-yellow-500" />
            <span>
              {cacheStats.entries} entrées · {Math.round(cacheStats.hitRate * 100)}% hits
            </span>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Liste des activités */}
      {entries.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground/60 italic py-1">
          Aucune activité — lancez une analyse
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-0.5">
          {entries.map((entry, idx) => (
            <div
              key={entry.id}
              className={cn(
                'flex items-start gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 rounded text-[11px] transition-opacity',
                idx === 0 ? 'bg-muted/40' : 'opacity-60 hover:opacity-80',
                entry.status === 'running' && 'bg-blue-500/5 opacity-100'
              )}
            >
              {statusIcon(entry.status)}
              <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1 flex-wrap">
                  <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate">{entry.label}</span>
                  <span className={cn('text-[10px] font-mono shrink-0', statusColor(entry.status))}>
                    {statusLabel(entry.status)}
                  </span>
                  {durationBadge(entry) && (
                    <span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-muted-foreground shrink-0">
                      {durationBadge(entry)}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
                {entry.detail && (
                  <div className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate mt-0.5">
                    {entry.detail}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

```
